              Innovative Education
             </h3>
            </div>
            <div class="home_feature_item_media">
             <span class="lazy_image_wrapper home_feature_item_image_wrapper">
              <img alt="" class="js-lazy js-lazyload home_feature_item_image" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://www.adelphi.edu/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/0110-300x200.jpg" data-srcset="https://www.adelphi.edu/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/0110-740x494.jpg 740w, https://www.adelphi.edu/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/0110-500x334.jpg 500w, https://www.adelphi.edu/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/0110-300x200.jpg 300w" src="https://www.adelphi.edu/wp-content/themes/primary/dist/images/placeholder.png?h=baae77a8"/>

We’re committed to academic excellence at every level: dedicated faculty, outstanding facilities, and meaningful real-world experiences through internships, independent research and international travel.

             <noscript>
              <img alt="" class="home_feature_item_image" sizes="100vw" src="https://www.adelphi.edu/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/Copy-of-Copy-of-0028-1-300x200.jpg" srcset="https://www.adelphi.edu/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/Copy-of-Copy-of-0028-1-740x494.jpg 740w, https://www.adelphi.edu/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/Copy-of-Copy-of-0028-1-500x334.jpg 500w, https://www.adelphi.edu/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/Copy-of-Copy-of-0028-1-300x200.jpg 300w"/>

            <div class="home_feature_item_body">
             <span class="home_feature_item_text">
              We value the richness in human differences and celebrate our exceptional diversity in many ways. Our warm welcome for different cultures, ages, ethnicities, genders and abilities has earned us national recognitions from the Campus Pride Index, Military FriendlyⓇ Schools, and the National Association of Diversity Officers.
             </span>
             <a class="home_feature_item_link" href="https://www.adelphi.edu/diversity-equity-inclusion/">

            <div class="statistics_featured_item_body">
             <span aria-hidden="true" class="statistics_featured_item_stat">
              Career Development
             </span>
             <div class="statistics_featured_item_description">
              <span class="featured_stat">
               Career Development
              </span>
              <span class="featured_label">
               Adelphi is one of 23 New York institutions named a Career Development College of Distinction for our superior ability to create strategic career plans and equip our students with the skills necessary to succeed after graduation.
              </span>
              <a class="statistics_featured_item_link" href="https://www.adelphi.edu/career-center/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
               <span class="statistics_featured_item_link_inner">
                <span class="statistics_featured_item_link_label">
                 Excellence in Career Support
                </span>
                <span aria-hidden="true" class="statistics_featured_item_link_icon">
                 <span class="statistics_featured_item_link_icon_inner">
                  <svg class="icon icon_arrow_right">
                   <use xlink:href="https://www.adelphi.edu/wp-content/themes/primary/dist/icons/icons.svg?h=3307b56a#arrow_right">
                   </use>
                  </svg>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </a>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="statistics_listing js-carousel" data-carousel-options='{"contained": false, "show": {"740px": 2, "980px": 1, "1220px": 2}}'>
            <div class="statistics_listing_item">

          <div class="flex_callout_body fs-lg-10 fs-xl-8">
           <h2 class="flex_callout_header">
            Driven by curiosity. Driven to succeed.
           </h2>
           <div class="flex_callout_description">
            Adelphi faculty contribute to their fields of study through research and creative work. Graduate and doctoral students embark on intensive projects in their discipline. And our undergrads have unparalleled opportunities to gain research experience.
           </div>

	function closePopup() {
		$CurrentTrigger.attr("aria-expanded", "false");
		$MenuControl.removeClass("open");
		$(".js-quick-links-panel").attr("aria-hidden", "true");
		$(".js-quick-links-panel-link").attr("tabindex", "-1");
	}
